## AcceptAllCertificatePolicy

服务器证书认证, For 1.1

### CheckValidationResult(srvPoint, certificate, request, certificateProblem)

服务器证书认证, For 1.1

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| srvPoint | *System.Net.ServicePoint*<br> |
| certificate | *System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate*<br> |
| request | *System.Net.WebRequest*<br> |
| certificateProblem | *System.Int32*<br> |

#### Returns

服务器证书认证, For 2.0

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |

| chain | *System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Chain*<br> |
| errors | *System.Net.Security.SslPolicyErrors*<br> |

#### Returns

## AdoHelper

The AdoHelper class is intended to encapsulate high performance, scalable best practices for common data access uses. It uses the Abstract Factory pattern to be easily extensible to any ADO.NET provider. The current implementation provides helpers for SQL Server, ODBC, OLEDB, and Oracle.

### AddUpdateEventHandlers(dataAdapter, rowUpdatingHandler, rowUpdatedHandler)

Provider specific code to set up the updating/ed event handlers used by UpdateDataset

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| dataAdapter | *System.Data.IDbDataAdapter*<br>DataAdapter to attach the event handlers to |
| rowUpdatingHandler | *Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.RowUpdatingHandler*<br>The handler to be called when a row is updating |
| rowUpdatedHandler | *Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.RowUpdatedHandler*<br>The handler to be called when a row is updated |


## AdoConnectionOwnership

This enum is used to indicate whether the connection was provided by the caller, or created by AdoHelper, so that we can set the appropriate CommandBehavior when calling ExecuteReader()

### External

Connection is owned and managed by the caller

### Internal

Connection is owned and managed by ADOHelper

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.AreParameterValuesIDataParameters(parameterValues, iDataParameterValues)

Check to see if the parameter values passed to the helper are, in fact, IDataParameters.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| parameterValues | *System.Object[]*<br>Array of parameter values passed to helper |
| iDataParameterValues | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>new array of IDataParameters built from parameter values |

#### Returns

True if the parameter values are IDataParameters

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.AssignParameterValues(commandParameters, dataRow)

This method assigns dataRow column values to an array of IDataParameters

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>Array of IDataParameters to be assigned values |
| dataRow | *System.Data.DataRow*<br>The dataRow used to hold the stored procedure's parameter values |

*System.InvalidOperationException:* Thrown if any of the parameter names are invalid.

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.AssignParameterValues(commandParameters, parameterValues)

This method assigns an array of values to an array of IDataParameters

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>Array of IDataParameters to be assigned values |
| parameterValues | *System.Object[]*<br>Array of objects holding the values to be assigned |

*System.ArgumentException:* Thrown if an incorrect number of parameters are passed.

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.AssignParameterValues(commandParameters, dataRow)

This method assigns dataRow column values to an IDataParameterCollection

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameterCollection*<br>The IDataParameterCollection to be assigned values |
| dataRow | *System.Data.DataRow*<br>The dataRow used to hold the stored procedure's parameter values |

*System.InvalidOperationException:* Thrown if any of the parameter names are invalid.

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.AttachParameters(command, commandParameters)

This method is used to attach array of IDataParameters to an IDbCommand. This method will assign a value of DbNull to any parameter with a direction of InputOutput and a value of null. This behavior will prevent default values from being used, but this will be the less common case than an intended pure output parameter (derived as InputOutput) where the user provided no input value.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| command | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>The command to which the parameters will be added |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>An array of IDataParameterParameters to be added to command |

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if command is null.

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.CacheParameterSet(connection, commandText, commandParameters)

Add parameter array to the cache

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.IDbConnection*<br>A valid IDbConnection |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or SQL command |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>An array of IDataParameters to be cached |

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.CacheParameterSet(connectionString, commandText, commandParameters)

Add parameter array to the cache

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>A valid connection string for an IDbConnection |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or SQL command |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>An array of IDataParameters to be cached |

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.CacheParameterSetInternal(connection, commandText, commandParameters)

Add parameter array to the cache

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.IDbConnection*<br>A valid IDbConnection |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or SQL command |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>An array of IDataParameters to be cached |

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.CheckForReturnValueParameter(parameterValues)

Checks for the existence of a return value parameter in the parametervalues

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| parameterValues | *System.Object[]*<br>An array of objects to be assigned as the input values of the stored procedure |

#### Returns

true if the parameterValues contains a return value parameter, false otherwise

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.CleanParameterSyntax(command)

This method cleans up the parameter syntax for the provider

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| command | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>The IDbCommand containing the parameters to clean up. |

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.ClearCommand(command)

This method clears (if necessary) the connection, transaction, command type and parameters from the provided command

#### Remarks

Not implemented here because the behavior of this method differs on each data provider.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| command | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>The IDbCommand to be cleared |

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.CreateCommand(connection, commandText, commandType, commandParameters)

Simplify the creation of an IDbCommand object by allowing a stored procedure and optional parameters to be provided

#### Example


```

            IDbCommand command = helper.CreateCommand(conn, "AddCustomer", "CustomerID", "CustomerName");
            
```


| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.IDbConnection*<br>A valid IDbConnection object |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>A valid SQL statement |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>A System.Data.CommandType |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>The parameters for the SQL statement |

#### Returns

A valid IDbCommand object

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.CreateCommand(connection, spName, sourceColumns)

Simplify the creation of an IDbCommand object by allowing a stored procedure and optional parameters to be provided

#### Example


```

            IDbCommand command = helper.CreateCommand(conn, "AddCustomer", "CustomerID", "CustomerName");
            
```


| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.IDbConnection*<br>A valid IDbConnection object |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| sourceColumns | *System.String[]*<br>An array of string to be assigned as the source columns of the stored procedure parameters |

#### Returns

A valid IDbCommand object

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if spName is null

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if connection is null

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.CreateCommand(connectionString, commandText, commandType, commandParameters)

Simplify the creation of an IDbCommand object by allowing a stored procedure and optional parameters to be provided

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>A valid connection string for an IDbConnection |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>A valid SQL statement |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>A System.Data.CommandType |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>The parameters for the SQL statement |

#### Returns

A valid IDbCommand object

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.CreateCommand(connectionString, spName, sourceColumns)

Simplify the creation of an IDbCommand object by allowing a stored procedure and optional parameters to be provided

#### Example


```

            IDbCommand command = helper.CreateCommand(conn, "AddCustomer", "CustomerID", "CustomerName");
            
```


| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>A valid connection string for an IDbConnection |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| sourceColumns | *System.String[]*<br>An array of string to be assigned as the source columns of the stored procedure parameters |

#### Returns

A valid IDbCommand object

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if connectionString is null

*System.InvalidOperationException:* Thrown if any of the IDataParameters.ParameterNames are null, or if the parameter count does not match the number of values supplied

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if spName is null

*System.ArgumentException:* Thrown if the parameter count does not match the number of values supplied

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.CreateHelper(providerAssembly, providerType)

Create an AdoHelper for working with a specific provider (i.e. Sql, Odbc, OleDb, Oracle)

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| providerAssembly | *System.String*<br>Assembly containing the specified helper subclass |
| providerType | *System.String*<br>Specific type of the provider |

#### Returns

An AdoHelper instance of the specified type

#### Example


```

            AdoHelper helper = AdoHelper.CreateHelper("GotDotNet.ApplicationBlocks.Data", "GotDotNet.ApplicationBlocks.Data.OleDb");
            
```


### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.CreateHelper(providerAlias)

Create an AdoHelper instance for working with a specific provider by using a providerAlias specified in the App.Config file.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| providerAlias | *System.String*<br>The alias to look up |

#### Returns

An AdoHelper instance of the specified type

#### Example


```

            AdoHelper helper = AdoHelper.CreateHelper("OracleHelper");
            
```


### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.DeriveParameters(cmd)

Calls the CommandBuilder.DeriveParameters method for the specified provider, doing any setup and cleanup necessary

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| cmd | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>The IDbCommand referencing the stored procedure from which the parameter information is to be derived. The derived parameters are added to the Parameters collection of the IDbCommand. |

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.DiscoverSpParameterSet(connection, spName, includeReturnValueParameter)

Resolve at run time the appropriate set of IDataParameters for a stored procedure

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.IDbConnection*<br>A valid IDbConnection object |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| includeReturnValueParameter | *System.Boolean*<br>Whether or not to include their return value parameter |

#### Returns

The parameter array discovered.

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if spName is null

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if connection is null

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.ExecuteDataset(command)

Execute an IDbCommand (that returns a resultset) against the database specified in the connection string.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| command | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>The IDbCommand object to use |

#### Returns

A DataSet containing the resultset generated by the command

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if command is null.

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.ExecuteDataset(connection, commandType, commandText, commandParameters)

Execute an IDbCommand (that returns a resultset) against the specified IDbConnection using the provided parameters.

#### Example


```

            DataSet ds = helper.ExecuteDataset(conn, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders", new IDataParameter("@prodid", 24));
            
```


| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.IDbConnection*<br>A valid IDbConnection |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or SQL command |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>An array of IDataParameters used to execute the command |

#### Returns

A DataSet containing the resultset generated by the command

*System.InvalidOperationException:* Thrown if any of the IDataParameters.ParameterNames are null, or if the parameter count does not match the number of values supplied

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if commandText is null

*System.ArgumentException:* Thrown if the parameter count does not match the number of values supplied

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if connection is null

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.ExecuteDataset(connection, commandType, commandText)

Execute an IDbCommand (that returns a resultset and takes no parameters) against the provided IDbConnection.

#### Example


```

            DataSet ds = helper.ExecuteDataset(conn, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders");
            
```


| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.IDbConnection*<br>A valid IDbConnection |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or SQL command |

#### Returns

A DataSet containing the resultset generated by the command

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if commandText is null

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if connection is null

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.ExecuteDataset(connection, spName, parameterValues)

Execute a stored procedure via an IDbCommand (that returns a resultset) against the specified IDbConnection using the provided parameter values. This method will query the database to discover the parameters for the stored procedure (the first time each stored procedure is called), and assign the values based on parameter order.

#### Remarks

This method provides no access to output parameters or the stored procedure's return value parameter.

#### Example


```

            DataSet ds = helper.ExecuteDataset(conn, "GetOrders", 24, 36);
            
```


| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.IDbConnection*<br>A valid IDbConnection |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| parameterValues | *System.Object[]*<br>An array of objects to be assigned as the input values of the stored procedure |

#### Returns

A DataSet containing the resultset generated by the command

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if spName is null

*System.ArgumentException:* Thrown if the parameter count does not match the number of values supplied

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if connection is null

an IDataReader containing the resultset generated by the command

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if commandText is null

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.ExecuteReader(connection, transaction, commandType, commandText, commandParameters, connectionOwnership)

Create and prepare an IDbCommand, and call ExecuteReader with the appropriate CommandBehavior.

#### Remarks

If we created and opened the connection, we want the connection to be closed when the DataReader is closed. If the caller provided the connection, we want to leave it to them to manage.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.IDbConnection*<br>A valid IDbConnection, on which to execute this command |
| transaction | *System.Data.IDbTransaction*<br>A valid IDbTransaction, or 'null' |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or SQL command |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>An array of IDataParameters to be associated with the command or 'null' if no parameters are required |
| connectionOwnership | *Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.AdoConnectionOwnership*<br>Indicates whether the connection parameter was provided by the caller, or created by AdoHelper |

#### Returns

IDataReader containing the results of the command

*System.InvalidOperationException:* Thrown if any of the IDataParameters.ParameterNames are null, or if the parameter count does not match the number of values supplied

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if commandText is null

*System.ArgumentException:* Thrown if the parameter count does not match the number of values supplied

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if connection is null

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.ExecuteReader(connection, spName, parameterValues)

Execute a stored procedure via an IDbCommand (that returns a resultset) against the specified IDbConnection using the provided parameter values. This method will query the database to discover the parameters for the stored procedure (the first time each stored procedure is called), and assign the values based on parameter order.

#### Remarks

This method provides no access to output parameters or the stored procedure's return value parameter.

#### Example


```

            IDataReader dr = helper.ExecuteReader(conn, "GetOrders", 24, 36);
            
```


| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.IDbConnection*<br>A valid IDbConnection |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| parameterValues | *System.Object[]*<br>An array of objects to be assigned as the input values of the stored procedure |

#### Returns

an IDataReader containing the resultset generated by the command

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if spName is null

*System.ArgumentException:* Thrown if the parameter count does not match the number of values supplied

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if connection is null

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.ExecuteReader(transaction, commandType, commandText, commandParameters)

Execute an IDbCommand (that returns a resultset) against the specified IDbTransaction using the provided parameters.

#### Example


```

            IDataReader dr = helper.ExecuteReader(trans, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders", new IDataParameter("@prodid", 24));
            
```


| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| transaction | *System.Data.IDbTransaction*<br>A valid IDbTransaction |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or SQL command |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>An array of IDataParameters used to execute the command |

#### Returns

A IDataReader containing the resultset generated by the command

| transaction | *System.Data.IDbTransaction*<br>A valid IDbTransaction |

| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or SQL command using "FOR XML AUTO" |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>An array of IDataParameters used to execute the command |

#### Returns

An XmlReader containing the resultset generated by the command

*System.InvalidOperationException:* Thrown if any of the IDataParameters.ParameterNames are null, or if the parameter count does not match the number of values supplied

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if commandText is null

*System.ArgumentException:* Thrown if the parameter count does not match the number of values supplied

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if transaction is null

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if transaction.Connection is null

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.ExecuteXmlReader(transaction, commandType, commandText)

Execute an IDbCommand (that returns a resultset and takes no parameters) against the provided IDbTransaction.

#### Example


```

            XmlReader r = helper.ExecuteXmlReader(tran, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders");
            
```


| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| transaction | *System.Data.IDbTransaction*<br>A valid IDbTransaction |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or SQL command using "FOR XML AUTO" |

#### Returns

An XmlReader containing the resultset generated by the command

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.ExecuteXmlReader(transaction, spName, parameterValues)

Execute a stored procedure via an IDbCommand (that returns a resultset) against the specified IDbTransaction using the provided parameter values. This method will query the database to discover the parameters for the stored procedure (the first time each stored procedure is called), and assign the values based on parameter order.

#### Remarks

This method provides no access to output parameters or the stored procedure's return value parameter.

#### Example


```

            XmlReader r = helper.ExecuteXmlReader(trans, "GetOrders", 24, 36);
            
```


| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| transaction | *System.Data.IDbTransaction*<br>A valid IDbTransaction |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure using "FOR XML AUTO" |
| parameterValues | *System.Object[]*<br>An array of objects to be assigned as the input values of the stored procedure |

#### Returns

An XmlReader containing the resultset generated by the command

*System.InvalidOperationException:* Thrown if any of the IDataParameters.ParameterNames are null, or if the parameter count does not match the number of values supplied

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if spName is null

*System.ArgumentException:* Thrown if the parameter count does not match the number of values supplied

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if transaction is null

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if transaction.Connection is null

An XmlReader containing the resultset generated by the command

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if command is null.

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.m_rowUpdated

Internal handler used for bubbling up the event to the user

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.m_rowUpdating

Internal handler used for bubbling up the event to the user

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.PrepareCommand(command, connection, transaction, commandType, commandText, commandParameters, mustCloseConnection)

This method opens (if necessary) and assigns a connection, transaction, command type and parameters to the provided command

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| command | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>The IDbCommand to be prepared |
| connection | *System.Data.IDbConnection*<br>A valid IDbConnection, on which to execute this command |
| transaction | *System.Data.IDbTransaction*<br>A valid IDbTransaction, or 'null' |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or SQL command |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>An array of IDataParameters to be associated with the command or 'null' if no parameters are required |
| mustCloseConnection | *System.Boolean@*<br>`true` if the connection was opened by the method, otherwose is false. |

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if command is null.

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if commandText is null.

| Name | Description |

#### Returns

An IDbCommand object

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.UpdateDataset(insertCommand, deleteCommand, updateCommand, dataSet, tableName, rowUpdatingHandler, rowUpdatedHandler)

Executes the IDbCommand for each inserted, updated, or deleted row in the DataSet also implementing RowUpdating and RowUpdated Event Handlers

#### Example


```

            RowUpdatingEventHandler rowUpdatingHandler = new RowUpdatingEventHandler( OnRowUpdating ); 
            RowUpdatedEventHandler rowUpdatedHandler = new RowUpdatedEventHandler( OnRowUpdated ); 
            helper.UpdateDataSet(sqlInsertCommand, sqlDeleteCommand, sqlUpdateCommand, dataSet, "Order", rowUpdatingHandler, rowUpdatedHandler); 
            
```


| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| insertCommand | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>A valid SQL statement or stored procedure to insert new records into the data source |
| deleteCommand | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>A valid SQL statement or stored procedure to delete records from the data source |
| updateCommand | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>A valid SQL statement or stored procedure used to update records in the data source |
| dataSet | *System.Data.DataSet*<br>The DataSet used to update the data source |
| tableName | *System.String*<br>The DataTable used to update the data source. |
| rowUpdatingHandler | *Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.RowUpdatingHandler*<br>RowUpdatingEventHandler |
| rowUpdatedHandler | *Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.RowUpdatedHandler*<br>RowUpdatedEventHandler |

### Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.UpdateDataset(insertCommand, deleteCommand, updateCommand, dataSet, tableName)

Executes the respective command for each inserted, updated, or deleted row in the DataSet.

#### Example


```

            helper.UpdateDataset(conn, insertCommand, deleteCommand, updateCommand, dataSet, "Order");
            
```


| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| insertCommand | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>A valid SQL statement or stored procedure to insert new records into the data source |
| deleteCommand | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>A valid SQL statement or stored procedure to delete records from the data source |
| updateCommand | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>A valid SQL statement or stored procedure used to update records in the data source |
| dataSet | *System.Data.DataSet*<br>The DataSet used to update the data source |
| tableName | *System.String*<br>The DataTable used to update the data source. |


## ADOHelperParameterCache

ADOHelperParameterCache provides functions to leverage a static cache of procedure parameters, and the ability to discover parameters for stored procedures at run-time.

### CacheParameterSet(connectionString, commandText, commandParameters)

Add parameter array to the cache

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>A valid connection string for an IDbConnection |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or SQL command |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br>An array of IDataParameters to be cached |

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if commandText is null

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if connectionString is null

### CloneParameters(originalParameters)

Deep copy of cached IDataParameter array

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| originalParameters | *System.Data.IDataParameter[]*<br> |

#### Returns



### GetCachedParameterSet(connectionString, commandText)

Retrieve a parameter array from the cache

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>A valid connection string for an IDbConnection |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or SQL command |

#### Returns

An array of IDataParameters

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if commandText is null

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if connectionString is null


## DAABSectionHandler

This class is for reading the 'daabProvider' section of the App.Config file

### Create(parent, configContext, section)

Evaluates the given XML section and returns a Hashtable that contains the results of the evaluation.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| parent | *System.Object*<br>The configuration settings in a corresponding parent configuration section. |
| configContext | *System.Object*<br>An HttpConfigurationContext when Create is called from the ASP.NET configuration system. Otherwise, this parameter is reserved and is a null reference (Nothing in Visual Basic). |
| section | *System.Xml.XmlNode*<br>The XmlNode that contains the configuration information to be handled. Provides direct access to the XML contents of the configuration section. |

#### Returns

A Hashtable that contains the section's configuration settings.

## Odbc

The Odbc class is intended to encapsulate high performance, scalable best practices for common uses of the Odbc ADO.NET provider. It is created using the abstract factory in AdoHelper

### Constructor

Create an Odbc Helper. Needs to be a default constructor so that the Factory can create it

### AddUpdateEventHandlers(dataAdapter, rowUpdatingHandler, rowUpdatedHandler)

Provider specific code to set up the updating/ed event handlers used by UpdateDataset

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| dataAdapter | *System.Data.IDbDataAdapter*<br>DataAdapter to attach the event handlers to |
| rowUpdatingHandler | *Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.RowUpdatingHandler*<br>The handler to be called when a row is updating |
| rowUpdatedHandler | *Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.RowUpdatedHandler*<br>The handler to be called when a row is updated |

### CleanParameterSyntax(command)

This cleans up the parameter syntax for an ODBC call. This was split out from PrepareCommand so that it could be called independently.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| command | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>An IDbCommand object containing the CommandText to clean. |

### DeriveParameters(cmd)

Calls the CommandBuilder.DeriveParameters method for the specified provider, doing any setup and cleanup necessary

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| cmd | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>The IDbCommand referencing the stored procedure from which the parameter information is to be derived. The derived parameters are added to the Parameters collection of the IDbCommand. |

### ExecuteXmlReader(command)

Execute an IDbCommand (that returns a resultset) against the provided IDbConnection.

#### Example


```

            XmlReader r = helper.ExecuteXmlReader(command);
            
```


| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| command | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>The IDbCommand to execute |

#### Returns

An XmlReader containing the resultset generated by the command

### GetBlobParameter(connection, p)

Handle any provider-specific issues with BLOBs here by "washing" the IDataParameter and returning a new one that is set up appropriately for the provider.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.IDbConnection*<br>The IDbConnection to use in cleansing the parameter |
| p | *System.Data.IDataParameter*<br>The parameter before cleansing |

#### Returns

The parameter after it's been cleansed.

### GetConnection(connectionString)

Returns an OdbcConnection object for the given connection string

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>The connection string to be used to create the connection |

#### Returns

An OdbcConnection object

### GetDataAdapter

Returns an OdbcDataAdapter object

#### Returns

The OdbcDataAdapter

### GetDataParameters(size)

Returns an array of OdbcParameters of the specified size

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| size | *System.Int32*<br>size of the array |

#### Returns

The array of OdbcParameters

### GetParameter

Returns an OdbcParameter object

#### Returns

The OdbcParameter object

### RowUpdated(obj, e)

Handles the RowUpdated event

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| obj | *System.Object*<br>The object that published the event |
| e | *System.Data.Odbc.OdbcRowUpdatedEventArgs*<br>The OdbcRowUpdatedEventArgs |

### RowUpdating(obj, e)

Handles the RowUpdating event

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| obj | *System.Object*<br>The object that published the event |
| e | *System.Data.Odbc.OdbcRowUpdatingEventArgs*<br>The OdbcRowUpdatingEventArgs |

## ProviderAlias

This class is for reading the 'ProviderAlias' tag from the 'daabProviders' section of the App.Config file

### Constructor(assemblyName, typeName)

Constructor required by IConfigurationSectionHandler

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| assemblyName | *System.String*<br>The Assembly where this provider can be found |
| typeName | *System.String*<br>The type of the provider |

### AssemblyName

Returns the Assembly name for this provider

#### Value

The Assembly name for the specified provider

### TypeName

Returns the type name of this provider

#### Value

The type name of the specified provider

### Data4Net.Ado.SqlDeriveParameters.GetParameterDirection(oledbDirection)

Converts the OleDb parameter direction

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| oledbDirection | *System.Int16*<br>The integer parameter direction |

#### Returns

A ParameterDirection

### Data4Net.Ado.SqlDeriveParameters.GetProcedureTokens(procedure, server, database, owner)

Tokenize the procedure string

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| procedure | *System.String@*<br>The procedure name |
| server | *System.String@*<br>The server name |
| database | *System.String@*<br>The database name |
| owner | *System.String@*<br>The owner name |

### Data4Net.Ado.SqlDeriveParameters.GetSqlDbType(paramType, typeName)

Convert OleDbType to SQlDbType

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| paramType | *System.Int16*<br>The OleDbType to convert |
| typeName | *System.String*<br>The typeName to convert for items such as Money and SmallMoney which both map to OleDbType.Currency |

#### Returns

The converted SqlDbType

### Data4Net.Ado.SqlDeriveParameters.IsEmptyString(str)

Checks for an empty string

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| str | *System.String*<br>String to check |

#### Returns

boolean value indicating whether string is empty

### Data4Net.Ado.SqlDeriveParameters.ParseGroupNumber(procedure)

Checks to see if the stored procedure being called is part of a group, then gets the group number if necessary

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| procedure | *System.String@*<br>Stored procedure being called. This method may change this parameter by removing the group number if it exists. |

#### Returns

the group number

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |

## MemcachedClient

Memcached client main class. Use the static methods Setup and GetInstance to setup and get an instance of the client for use.

### Add(key, value, expiry)

This method corresponds to the "add" command in the memcached protocol. It will set the given key to the given value only if the key does not already exist. Using the overloads it is possible to specify an expiry time, either relative as a TimeSpan or absolute as a DateTime. It is also possible to specify a custom hash to override server selection. This method returns true if the value was successfully added.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| key | *System.String*<br> |
| value | *System.Object*<br> |
| expiry | *System.DateTime*<br> |

#### Returns

This method returns true if the value was successfully added.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| key | *System.String*<br> |
| value | *System.Object*<br> |
| expiry | *System.TimeSpan*<br> |

#### Returns

This method returns true if the value was successfully added.

### Append(key, value, hash)

This method corresponds to the "append" command in the memcached protocol. It will append the given value to the given key, if the key already exists. Modifying a key with this command will not change its expiry time. Using the overload it is possible to specify a custom hash to override server selection.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| key | *System.String*<br> |
| value | *System.Object*<br> |
| hash | *System.UInt32*<br> |

#### Returns

Modifying a key with this command will not change its expiry time. Using the overload it is possible to specify a custom hash to override server selection.

### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.checkKey(key)

Private key-checking method. Throws an exception if the key does not conform to memcached protocol requirements: It may not contain whitespace, it may not be null or empty, and it may not be longer than 250 characters.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| key | *System.String*<br>The key to check. |

### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.CompressionThreshold

If an object being stored is larger in bytes than the compression threshold, it will internally be compressed before begin stored, and it will transparently be decompressed when retrieved. Only strings, byte arrays and objects can be compressed. The default value is 1048576 bytes = 1MB.

### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.ConnectTimeout

The connect timeout is used to determine how long the client should wait for a connection to be established, specified in milliseconds. The default value is 2000.

### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.Decrement(key, value, hash)

This method corresponds to the "decr" command in the memcached protocol. It will decrease the item with the given value and return the new value. If the new value would be less than 0, it will be set to 0, and the method will return 0. It will return null if the item did not exist, was not stored properly as per the SetCounter method, or if it was not able to successfully retrieve the item.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| key | *System.String*<br> |
| value | *System.UInt64*<br> |
| hash | *System.UInt32*<br> |

#### Returns



### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.Decrement(key, value)

This method corresponds to the "decr" command in the memcached protocol. It will decrease the item with the given value and return the new value. If the new value would be less than 0, it will be set to 0, and the method will return 0. It will return null if the item did not exist, was not stored properly as per the SetCounter method, or if it was not able to successfully retrieve the item.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| key | *System.String*<br> |
| value | *System.UInt64*<br> |

#### Returns

### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.Delete(key, delay)

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| key | *System.String*<br> |
| delay | *System.DateTime*<br> |

#### Returns

### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.FlushAll

This method corresponds to the "flush_all" command in the memcached protocol. When this method is called, it will send the flush command to all servers, thereby deleting all items on all servers. Use the overloads to set a delay for the flushing. If the parameter staggered is set to true, the client will increase the delay for each server, i.e. the first will flush after delay*0, the second after delay*1, the third after delay*2, etc. If set to false, all servers will flush after the same delay. It returns true if the command was successful on all servers.

#### Returns



### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.FlushAll(delay, staggered)

This method corresponds to the "flush_all" command in the memcached protocol. When this method is called, it will send the flush command to all servers, thereby deleting all items on all servers. Use the overloads to set a delay for the flushing. If the parameter staggered is set to true, the client will increase the delay for each server, i.e. the first will flush after delay*0, the second after delay*1, the third after delay*2, etc. If set to false, all servers will flush after the same delay. It returns true if the command was successful on all servers.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| delay | *System.TimeSpan*<br> |
| staggered | *System.Boolean*<br> |

#### Returns



### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.FlushAll(delay)

This method corresponds to the "flush_all" command in the memcached protocol. When this method is called, it will send the flush command to all servers, thereby deleting all items on all servers. Use the overloads to set a delay for the flushing. If the parameter staggered is set to true, the client will increase the delay for each server, i.e. the first will flush after delay*0, the second after delay*1, the third after delay*2, etc. If set to false, all servers will flush after the same delay. It returns true if the command was successful on all servers.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| delay | *System.TimeSpan*<br> |

#### Returns



### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.Get(key, hash)

This method corresponds to the "get" command in the memcached protocol. It will return the value for the given key. It will return null if the key did not exist, or if it was unable to retrieve the value. If given an array of keys, it will return a same-sized array of objects with the corresponding values. Use the overload to specify a custom hash to override server selection.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| key | *System.String*<br> |
| hash | *System.UInt32*<br> |

#### Returns



### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.Get(System.String)

This method corresponds to the "get" command in the memcached protocol. It will return the value for the given key. It will return null if the key did not exist, or if it was unable to retrieve the value. If given an array of keys, it will return a same-sized array of objects with the corresponding values. Use the overload to specify a custom hash to override server selection.

### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.Get(keys, hashes)

This method executes a multi-get. It will group the keys by server and execute a single get for each server, and combine the results. The returned object[] will have the same size as the given key array, and contain either null or a value at each position according to the key on that position.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| keys | *System.String[]*<br> |
| hashes | *System.UInt32[]*<br> |

#### Returns



### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.Get(keys)

This method executes a multi-get. It will group the keys by server and execute a single get for each server, and combine the results. The returned object[] will have the same size as the given key array, and contain either null or a value at each position according to the key on that position.

| keys | *System.String[]*<br> |

### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.KeyPrefix

If you specify a key prefix, it will be appended to all keys before they are sent to the memcached server. They key prefix is not used when calculating which server a key belongs to.

### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.MaxPoolSize

The max pool size determines how large the socket connection pool is allowed to grow. There can be more sockets in use than this amount, but when the extra sockets are returned, they will be destroyed. The default value is 10.

### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.MinPoolSize

The min pool size determines the number of sockets the socket pool will keep. Note that no sockets will be created on startup, only on use, so the socket pool will only contain this amount of sockets if the amount of simultaneous requests goes above it. The default value is 5.

### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.Prepend(key, value, hash)

This method corresponds to the "prepend" command in the memcached protocol. It will prepend the given value to the given key, if the key already exists. Modifying a key with this command will not change its expiry time. Using the overload it is possible to specify a custom hash to override server selection.

| Name | Description |

### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.Setup(name, servers)

Static method for creating an instance. This method will throw an exception if the name already exists.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| name | *System.String*<br>The name of the instance. |
| servers | *System.String[]*<br>A list of memcached servers in standard notation: host:port. If port is omitted, the default value of 11211 is used. Both IP addresses and host names are accepted, for example: "localhost", "127.0.0.1", "cache01.example.com:12345", "127.0.0.1:12345", etc. |

### Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.MemcachedClient.SocketRecycleAge

If the pool contains more than the minimum amount of sockets, and a socket is returned that is older than this recycle age that socket will be destroyed instead of put back in the pool. This allows the pool to shrink back to the min pool size after a peak in usage. The default value is 30 minutes.

## ModifiedFNV1_32

Modified Fowler-Noll-Vo hash, 32-bit version. http://home.comcast.net/~bretm/hash/6.html

### HashFinal



#### Returns




## PooledSocket

The PooledSocket class encapsulates a socket connection to a specified memcached server. It contains a buffered stream for communication, and methods for sending and retrieving data from the memcached server, as well as general memcached error checking.

### Close

This method closes the underlying stream and socket.

### Dispose

Disposing of a PooledSocket object in any way causes it to be returned to its SocketPool.

### IsAlive

Checks if the underlying socket and stream is connected and available.

### Read(System.Byte[])

Fills the given byte array with data from the socket.

### ReadLine

Reads from the socket until the sequence '\r\n' is encountered, and returns everything up to but not including that sequence as a UTF8-encoded string

### ReadResponse

Reads a response line from the socket, checks for general memcached errors, and returns the line. If an error is encountered, this method will throw an exception.

### Reset

Resets this PooledSocket by making sure the incoming buffer of the socket is empty. If there was any leftover data, this method return true.

### SkipUntilEndOfLine

Reads from the socket until the sequence '\r\n' is encountered.

### Write(System.Byte[])

Writes an array of bytes to the socket and flushes the stream.

### Write(System.String)

Writes a string to the socket encoded in UTF8 format.


## ServerPool

The ServerPool encapsulates a collection of memcached servers and the associated SocketPool objects. This class contains the server-selection logic, and contains methods for executing a block of code on a socket from the server corresponding to a given key.

### Constructor(System.String[])

Internal constructor. This method takes the array of hosts and sets up an internal list of socketpools.

### Execute\`\`1(System.UInt32,\`\`0,Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.UseSocket{\`\`0})

This method executes the given delegate on a socket from the server that corresponds to the given hash. If anything causes an error, the given defaultValue will be returned instead. This method takes care of disposing the socket properly once the delegate has executed.

### ExecuteAll(Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.UseSocket)

This method executes the given delegate on all servers.

### GetSocketPool(System.UInt32)

Given an item key hash, this method returns the socketpool which is closest on the server key continuum.


## SocketPool

The SocketPool encapsulates the list of PooledSockets against one specific host, and contains methods for acquiring or returning PooledSockets.

### Acquire

Gets a socket from the pool. If there are no free sockets, a new one will be created. If something goes wrong while creating the new socket, this pool's endpoint will be marked as dead and all subsequent calls to this method will return null until the retry interval has passed.

### deadEndPointSecondsUntilRetry

If the host stops responding, we mark it as dead for this amount of seconds, and we double this for each consecutive failed retry. If the host comes alive again, we reset this to 1 again.

### getEndPoint(System.String)

This method parses the given string into an IPEndPoint. If the string is malformed in some way, or if the host cannot be resolved, this method will throw an exception.

### Return(Data4Net.BeIT.MemCached.PooledSocket)

Returns a socket to the pool. If the socket is dead, it will be destroyed. If there are more than MaxPoolSize sockets in the pool, it will be destroyed. If there are less than MinPoolSize sockets in the pool, it will always be put back. If there are something inbetween those values, the age of the socket is checked. If it is older than the SocketRecycleAge, it is destroyed, otherwise it will be put back in the pool.

## CaseConvert

全角(SBC case)半角(DBC case)转换类（C#） 全角空格为12288，半角空格为32 其他字符半角(33-126)与全角(65281-65374)的对应关系是：均相差65248

### ToDBC(input)

转半角的函数(DBC case)

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| input | *System.String*<br>任意字符串 |

#### Returns

半角字符串

#### Remarks

全角空格为12288，半角空格为32 其他字符半角(33-126)与全角(65281-65374)的对应关系是：均相差65248

### ToSBC(input)

转全角的函数(SBC case)

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| input | *System.String*<br>任意字符串 |

#### Returns

全角字符串

#### Remarks

全角空格为12288，半角空格为32 其他字符半角(33-126)与全角(65281-65374)的对应关系是：均相差65248

## FormActionFixer

重载form中action的值, 可以支持http浏览提交到https上, 在BasePage中重载Render方法, 如下: protected override void Render(HtmlTextWriter writer) { writer = new FormActionFixer(writer, delegate(string value) { string orgUrl = value; Uri u = HttpContext.Current.Request.Url; if (u.Scheme.ToLower() == "http") { return FormActionFixerHelper.GetHttpsUrl(u, "443"); } return string.IsNullOrEmpty(orgUrl) ? u.ToString() : orgUrl; }); base.Render(writer); }

### Constructor(writer, getValue)



| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| writer | *System.IO.TextWriter*<br> |
| getValue | *Data4Net.Controls.Web.FormActionFixer.GetValueMethod*<br> |

### Constructor(writer, tagString, getValue)



| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| writer | *System.IO.TextWriter*<br> |
| tagString | *System.String*<br> |
| getValue | *Data4Net.Controls.Web.FormActionFixer.GetValueMethod*<br> |

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| value | *System.Object*<br> |

#### Returns

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| value | *System.Object*<br> |

#### Returns

### GetDateTime_Cn(value, defaultValue, minValue, maxValue, dpMinMaxMethod)

得到格式 yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss.fff 日期型, 是否补0、是否有月、日、时间、毫秒等都行, 至少必须含有一个数字的年份日期字符串 支持只要是按照 年 月 日 小时 分钟 秒 毫秒 排列的任何字符串，分隔符可以是 ' ', '-', ':', '.', '/', '\\', ',', '年', '月', '日'等所有非数字字符

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| value | *System.String*<br> |
| defaultValue | *System.DateTime*<br> |
| minValue | *System.DateTime*<br> |
| maxValue | *System.DateTime*<br> |
| dpMinMaxMethod | *Data4Net.DpMinMaxMethod*<br> |

#### Returns



### GetDateTime_Cn(value, defaultValue, minValue, maxValue)

得到格式 yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss.fff 日期型, 是否补0、是否有月、日、时间、毫秒等都行, 至少必须含有一个数字的年份日期字符串 支持只要是按照 年 月 日 小时 分钟 秒 毫秒 排列的任何字符串，分隔符可以是 ' ', '-', ':', '.', '/', '\\', ',', '年', '月', '日'等所有非数字字符

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| value | *System.String*<br> |
| defaultValue | *System.DateTime*<br> |
| minValue | *System.DateTime*<br> |
| maxValue | *System.DateTime*<br> |

#### Returns

### GetMsSqlServerDateTime(value)

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| value | *System.DateTime*<br> |

#### Returns



### GetMsSqlServerSmallDateTime(value)

得到一个Ms Sql Server中SmallDateTime范围的日期 (1900-01-01 00:00:00.000 / 2079-06-06 23:59:00.000) 超出范围返回 MinValue, 即 1900-01-01 00:00:00.000

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| value | *System.DateTime*<br> |

#### Returns



### GetUnixTicks(time)

根据时间获取标准Unix时间 Unix系统内核提供的基本时间服务是国际标准时间公元1970年1月1日00:00:00以来经过的秒数,这种秒数是以数据类型time_t表示的。 我们称它们为日历时间。日历时间包括时间和日期。

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| time | *System.DateTime*<br> |

#### Returns

## DKeyAes

基于MD5的动态Key加密解密AES算法 .Net 3.5 全新引入了 AesManaged 代替 RijndaelManaged; AesManaged and RijndaelManaged 差异见: http://blogs.msdn.com/b/shawnfa/archive/2006/10/09/the-differences-between-rijndael-and-aes.aspx 


## DKeyDes

基于MD5的动态Key加密解密DES算法 

### _keyChar

Key的字符集 (该字符长度大于256的部分无意义, 不会被使用到)

### _keyLength

Key长度

### _md5

MD5对象

### _md5Char

MD5格式字符串, {T}替换时间, 区分大小写, 如 aaa{T}bbbccc, 其中aaabbbccc为混淆码

### Constructor(keyChar, md5Char)

构造函数

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| keyChar | *System.String*<br>Key的字符集 如"0123456789" (该字符长度大于256的部分无意义, 不会被使用到) |
| md5Char | *System.String*<br>MD5格式字符串, {T}替换时间, 区分大小写, 如 aaa{T}bbbccc, 其中aaabbbccc为混淆码 |

### Decrypt(value, timeTicks)

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| value | *System.Byte[]*<br> |
| timeTicks | *System.String*<br> |

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| timeTicks | *System.String*<br> |

## DKeyMd5

基于MD5的1分钟动态Key类 

### _keyChar

Key的字符集 (该字符长度大于256的部分无意义, 不会被使用到)

### _keyLength

Key长度，必须在1-16之间（1,16包含）

### _md5

MD5对象

### _md5Char

MD5格式字符串, {T}替换时间 {V}替换值, 区分大小写, 如 aaa{T}bbb{V}ccc, 其中aaabbbccc为混淆码

### _timeStep

时间步长, 0-31536000(1年)

### Constructor(keyChar, keyLength, md5Char, timeStep)

构造函数

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| keyChar | *System.String*<br>Key的字符集 如"0123456789" (该字符长度大于256的部分无意义, 不会被使用到) |
| keyLength | *System.Int32*<br>Key长度，必须在1-16之间（1,16包含） |
| md5Char | *System.String*<br>MD5格式字符串, {T}替换时间 {V}替换值, 区分大小写, 如 aaa{T}bbb{V}ccc, 其中aaabbbccc为混淆码 |
| timeStep | *System.Int64*<br>时间步长, 单位毫秒, 建议0-31536000000(1年)之间(包含), 如60000 |

### CheckKey(value, code, steps, now, isLower, key)

验证当前时间Key

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| value | *System.String*<br> |
| code | *System.String*<br> |
| steps | *System.Int32*<br>前后几个步长, 建议取值范围0-10, 如3则表示输出当前步长和前后2次时间间隔的步长共7个key中是否包含这个输入的code |
| now | *System.DateTime*<br> |
| isLower | *System.Boolean*<br>是否忽略大小写 true忽略 false区分大小写 |
| key | *System.String@*<br> |

#### Returns



### CheckKey(value, code, steps, key)

验证当前时间Key, 默认当前时间, 默认忽略大小写比较

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| value | *System.String*<br> |
| code | *System.String*<br> |
| steps | *System.Int32*<br>前后几个步长, 建议取值范围0-10, 如3则表示输出当前步长和前后2次时间间隔的步长共7个key中是否包含这个输入的code |
| key | *System.String@*<br> |

#### Returns



### GetKey(value, now)

得到当前时间单个Key

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| value | *System.String*<br> |
| now | *System.DateTime*<br> |

#### Returns



### GetKey(value, steps, now)

得到任意时间, 任意几个Key

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| value | *System.String*<br> |
| steps | *System.Int32*<br>前后几个步长, 建议取值范围0-10, 如3则表示输出当前步长和前后3次时间间隔的步长共7个key |
| now | *System.DateTime*<br> |

#### Returns

多个Key, 每个生成的Key用英文字符逗号分割

### GetKey(value)

得到当前时间单个Key

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| value | *System.String*<br> |

#### Returns

## FilterRealProxy

FilterRealProxy类：一个真实代理, 拦截它所代理对象中方法的返回值，并对需要过滤的返回值进行过滤。 使用方法 public void xxx() { Class1 class1 = new Class1();//Class1必须从MarshalByRefObject继承 //以下是增加用来过滤的 FilterRealProxy proxy = new FilterRealProxy(class1); class1 = (Class1)proxy.GetTransparentProxy(); //以上是增加用来过滤的 string s = class1.Method1();//要过滤得方法Method1要加属性[StringFilter(FilterType.html)] } public class Class1 : MarshalByRefObject { [StringFilter(FilterType.Iframe)] [StringFilter(FilterType.Object)] public string Method1() { return ""; } }

### Constructor(target)



| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| target | *System.MarshalByRefObject*<br> |

### Filter(ReturnValue, MethodName)



| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| ReturnValue | *System.String*<br> |
| MethodName | *System.String*<br> |

#### Returns



### Invoke(msg)



| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| msg | *System.Runtime.Remoting.Messaging.IMessage*<br> |

#### Returns

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| obj | *System.Object*<br> |

#### Returns

### PostClientSubmitImage(urls, img, destImgFormat, addInfo, dataStr, timeout, userAgent, encodingName, resultSplit, errorSplit, result, error)

PostClient SubmitImage 

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| urls | *System.String*<br>支持多个URL, 英文字符逗号分割 |
| img | *System.Byte[]*<br>图片的二进制数据 |
| destImgFormat | *System.Drawing.Imaging.ImageFormat*<br>图片格式, 如System.Drawing.Imaging.ImageFormat.Jpeg |
| addInfo | *Data4Net.ImageAddInfo*<br>图片处理规范数据 |
| dataStr | *System.String*<br>img={IMG}&aa=1&bb=2&cc=3, 其中{IMG}将被替换成byte[] imgSave这个的Convert.ToBase64String()形式, {IMG}区分大写小 |
| timeout | *System.Int32*<br>20000 |
| userAgent | *System.String*<br>"User-Agent: Mozilla/4.0 (compatible; MSIE 6.0; Windows NT 5.2; .NET CLR 1.0.3705;)"; //模拟IE6 |
| encodingName | *System.String*<br>"utf-8" |
| resultSplit | *System.String*<br>当含有多个result时的分隔符 如 # |
| errorSplit | *System.String*<br>当含有多个error时的分隔符, 如 System.Environment.NewLine |
| result | *System.String@*<br> |
| error | *System.String@*<br> |

#### Returns

## IOCPSafeThreadPool

This class provides the ability to create a thread pool to manage work. The class abstracts the Win32 IOCompletionPort API so it requires the use of unmanaged code. Unfortunately the .NET framework does not provide this functionality

### Constructor(iMaxConcurrency, iMinThreadsInPool, iMaxThreadsInPool, pfnUserFunction)

Constructor

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| iMaxConcurrency | *System.Int32*<br>SimType: Max number of running threads allowed |
| iMinThreadsInPool | *System.Int32*<br>SimType: Min number of threads in the pool |
| iMaxThreadsInPool | *System.Int32*<br>SimType: Max number of threads in the pool |
| pfnUserFunction | *Data4Net.IOCPSafeThreadPool.USER_FUNCTION*<br>DelType: Reference to a function to call to perform work |

*System.Exception:* Unhandled Exception

### CloseHandle(System.Runtime.InteropServices.SafeHandle)

Win32Func: Closes an IO Completion Port Thread Pool

### CreateIoCompletionPort(System.IntPtr,System.IntPtr,System.IntPtr,System.UInt32)

Win32Func: Create an IO Completion Port Thread Pool

### DecActThreadsInPool

SimType: Decrement current number of active threads in the thread pool

### DecCurThreadsInPool

SimType: Decrement current number of threads in the thread pool

### DecCurWorkInPool

SimType: Decrement current number of Work posted in the thread pool

### Dispose

Called when the object will be shutdown. This function will wait for all of the work to be completed inside the queue before completing

### Finalize

Finalize called by the GC

### GetActThreadsInPool

SimType: The current number of active threads in the thread pool

### GetCriticalSection

RefType: A serialization object to protect the class state

### GetCurThreadsInPool

SimType: The current number of threads in the thread pool

### GetCurWorkInPool

SimType: The current number of Work posted in the thread pool

### GetHandle

SimType: Contains the IO Completion Port Thread Pool handle for this instance

### GetMaxConcurrency

SimType: The maximum number of threads that may be running at the same time

### GetMaxThreadsInPool

SimType: The maximum number of threads the thread pool maintains

### GetMinThreadsInPool

SimType: The minimal number of threads the thread pool maintains

### GetQueuedCompletionStatus(Microsoft.Win32.SafeHandles.SafeFileHandle,System.UInt32@,System.IntPtr@,System.IntPtr@,System.UInt32)

Win32Func: Waits on a context based event from an IO Completion Port Thread Pool. All threads in the pool wait in this Win32 Function

### GetUserFunction

DelType: A reference to a user specified function to be call by the thread pool

### IncActThreadsInPool

SimType: Increment current number of active threads in the thread pool

### IncCurThreadsInPool

SimType: Increment current number of threads in the thread pool

### IncCurWorkInPool

SimType: Increment current number of Work posted in the thread pool

### INIFINITE

SimTypeConst: This represents the Win32 INFINITE Macro

### INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE

SimTypeConst: This represents the Win32 Invalid Handle Value Macro

### IOCPFunction

IOCP Worker Function that calls the specified user function

### IsDisposed

SimType: Flag to indicate if the class is disposing

### PostEvent

IOCP Worker Function that calls the specified user function

*System.Exception:* Unhandled Exception

### PostEvent(obj)

IOCP Worker Function that calls the specified user function

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| obj | *Data4Net.IOCPData*<br>SimType: A value to be passed with the event |

*System.Exception:* Unhandled Exception

### PostQueuedCompletionStatus(Microsoft.Win32.SafeHandles.SafeFileHandle,System.UInt32,System.IntPtr,System.IntPtr)

Win32Func: Posts a context based event into an IO Completion Port Thread Pool

### SHUTDOWN_IOCPTHREAD

SimTypeConst: This tells the IOCP Function to shutdown


## USER_FUNCTION

DelType: This is the type of user function to be supplied for the thread pool

## IpHelper

IpHelper Class

### Int2Ip(ipCode)

Int2Ip, int to ip string 我们知道 IP地址就是给每个连接在Internet上的主机分配的一个32bit地址。 按照TCP/IP协议规定，IP地址用二进制来表示，每个IP地址长32bit，比特换算成字节，就是4个字节。 而c#中int32的数就是四个字节的，但是符号要占掉一位所以就不够了，但是无符号的 UInt32 就没有这样的问题。 所以理论上讲：UInt32是可以完整保存一个IP地址的。那下面的两个方法就是对IP与UInt32之间的互转换。

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| ipCode | *System.UInt32*<br> |

#### Returns



### Ip2Int(ipStr)

Ip2Int, ip string to int 我们知道 IP地址就是给每个连接在Internet上的主机分配的一个32bit地址。 按照TCP/IP协议规定，IP地址用二进制来表示，每个IP地址长32bit，比特换算成字节，就是4个字节。 而c#中int32的数就是四个字节的，但是符号要占掉一位所以就不够了，但是无符号的 UInt32 就没有这样的问题。 所以理论上讲：UInt32是可以完整保存一个IP地址的。那下面的两个方法就是对IP与UInt32之间的互转换。

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| ipStr | *System.String*<br> |

#### Returns



### IsIpV4(ipStr)

判断一个 IP String 是否是 IPV4 的格式

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| ipStr | *System.String*<br> |

#### Returns

### AsyncLogDataItem

### ToLogAsync(msg, levelKeyItem, logMark, logTime)

ToLog 2.0版本，建议使用, 异步版本 (目前性能不稳定，不推荐使用，在极高速情况下会有丢失日志的现象)

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| msg | *System.String*<br> |
| levelKeyItem | *System.String[]*<br> |
| logMark | *System.String*<br> |
| logTime | *System.DateTime*<br> |

#### Returns



### ToLogOnEndApp

当 Application 结束时把内存中的所有日志信息记录到文本中 如在 Application_End 或 Application_Disposed 中使用

#### Returns

### TidCurrent

当前线程TID AppDomain.GetCurrentThreadId()实际上调用的是WIN32 API，其返回的是该线程在windows中的ThreadId； Thread.ManagedThreadId 返回的是作为一个ManagedThread在.NET CLR中的ThreadId； 所以这和windows的ThreadId是完全不同的。

| webRequest | *System.Net.HttpWebRequest*<br>HttpWebRequest webRequest = (HttpWebRequest)WebRequest.Create(url); httpWebReq.UserAgent = @"Mozilla/4.0 (compatible; MSIE 6.0; Windows NT 5.1)" webRequest.Timeout = 5000; //解决HttpWebResponse无法获取cookie的解决办法, 需要在GetResponse()之前new CookieContainer() //msdn: 默认情况下，CookieContainer 为 null。 必须将 CookieContainer 对象分配给该属性以在由 GetResponse 方法返回的 HttpWebResponse 的 Cookies 属性中返回 Cookie。 //msdn: 为安全起见，默认情况下禁用 Cookie。 如果您希望使用 Cookie，请使用 CookieContainer 属性启用 Cookie。 webRequest.CookieContainer = new CookieContainer(); PS: 1. 解决HttpWebResponse无法获取cookie的解决办法, 需要在GetResponse()之前new CookieContainer() |

### GetWebResponse(webRequest)

通过HttpWebRequest得到WebResponse ex: webRequest = (HttpWebRequest)WebRequest.Create(url); webRequest.Timeout = timeout; //超时时间 //webRequest.UserAgent = "User-Agent: Mozilla/4.0 (compatible; MSIE 6.0; Windows NT 5.2; .NET CLR 1.0.3705;)"; //模拟IE6 webRequest.UserAgent = userAgent; //Post webRequest.Method = "POST"; Encoding encoding = Encoding.GetEncoding(encodingName); byte[] data = encoding.GetBytes(dataStr); webRequest.ContentType = "application/x-www-form-urlencoded"; webRequest.ContentLength = data.Length; // Send the data. Stream smreq = webRequest.GetRequestStream(); smreq.Write(data, 0, data.Length); smreq.Close(); webResponse = (HttpWebResponse)NetHelper.GetWebResponse(webRequest); using (StreamReader Reader = new StreamReader(webResponse.GetResponseStream(), Encoding.GetEncoding("utf-8"))) { result += Reader.ReadToEnd() + resultSplit; }

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| webRequest | *System.Net.HttpWebRequest*<br> |

#### Returns



### GetWebResponse(webRequest)

通过WebRequest得到WebResponse ex: webRequest = (HttpWebRequest)WebRequest.Create(url); webRequest.Timeout = timeout; //超时时间 //webRequest.UserAgent = "User-Agent: Mozilla/4.0 (compatible; MSIE 6.0; Windows NT 5.2; .NET CLR 1.0.3705;)"; //模拟IE6 webRequest.UserAgent = userAgent; //Post webRequest.Method = "POST"; Encoding encoding = Encoding.GetEncoding(encodingName); byte[] data = encoding.GetBytes(dataStr); webRequest.ContentType = "application/x-www-form-urlencoded"; webRequest.ContentLength = data.Length; // Send the data. Stream smreq = webRequest.GetRequestStream(); smreq.Write(data, 0, data.Length); smreq.Close(); webResponse = (HttpWebResponse)NetHelper.GetWebResponse(webRequest); using (StreamReader Reader = new StreamReader(webResponse.GetResponseStream(), Encoding.GetEncoding("utf-8"))) { result += Reader.ReadToEnd() + resultSplit; }

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| webRequest | *System.Net.WebRequest*<br> |

#### Returns

### PostUrlReturnByType(dataStr, type, encoding, webRequest)

Post string[] by url

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| dataStr | *System.String*<br> |
| type | *Data4Net.ReadTypeEnum*<br>0 ReadToEnd, 1 ReadLineFirst, 2 ReadLineArrayList |
| encoding | *System.Text.Encoding*<br>ex: GB2312,UTF-8 |
| webRequest | *System.Net.HttpWebRequest*<br>HttpWebRequest webRequest = (HttpWebRequest)WebRequest.Create(url); httpWebReq.UserAgent = @"Mozilla/4.0 (compatible; MSIE 6.0; Windows NT 5.1)" webRequest.Timeout = 5000; //解决HttpWebResponse无法获取cookie的解决办法, 需要在GetResponse()之前new CookieContainer() //msdn: 默认情况下，CookieContainer 为 null。 必须将 CookieContainer 对象分配给该属性以在由 GetResponse 方法返回的 HttpWebResponse 的 Cookies 属性中返回 Cookie。 //msdn: 为安全起见，默认情况下禁用 Cookie。 如果您希望使用 Cookie，请使用 CookieContainer 属性启用 Cookie。 webRequest.CookieContainer = new CookieContainer(); PS: 1. 解决HttpWebResponse无法获取cookie的解决办法, 需要在GetResponse()之前new CookieContainer() |

#### Returns

| toEamil | *System.String*<br>To email address |
| title | *System.String*<br>Title of email |
| content | *System.String*<br>Conent of email |
| isBodyHtml | *System.Boolean*<br>If mail's format is html, set this value to true |
| encodingName | *System.String*<br>mail encoding name |
| filePath | *System.String[]*<br>attachments path |
| attachs | *System.Net.Mail.Attachment[]*<br>attachments |
| isAddBoundary | *System.Boolean*<br>isAddBoundary |
| boundaryValue | *System.String*<br>boundaryValue |

### ReplaceUrlKeyToEmpty(url, key)

Replace Url Key To Empty, ex: key=aa http://aaa.com/aa.aspx?aa=aa -> http://aaa.com/aa.aspx http://aaa.com/aa.aspx?bb=bb&aa=aa -> http://aaa.com/aa.aspx?bb=bb http://aaa.com/aa.aspx?aa=aa&cc=cc -> http://aaa.com/aa.aspx?cc=cc http://aaa.com/aa.aspx?bb=bb&aa=aa&cc=cc -> http://aaa.com/aa.aspx?bb=bb&cc=cc http://aaa.com/aa.aspx?bb=vvv&aa=xxx&cc=yyy -> http://aaa.com/aa.aspx?bb=vvv&cc=yyy

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| url | *System.String*<br> |
| key | *System.String*<br> |

## SqlDataHelper

SqlDataHelper 的摘要说明


## SqlHelper

The SqlHelper class is intended to encapsulate high performance, scalable best practices for common uses of SqlClient

### CreateCommand(connection, commandText, commandType, commandParameters)

Simplify the creation of a Sql command object by allowing a stored procedure and optional parameters to be provided

#### Remarks

e.g.: SqlCommand command = CreateCommand(conn, "AddCustomer", "CustomerID", "CustomerName");

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection object |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>A valid SQL string to execute |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType to execute (i.e. StoredProcedure, Text) |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlParameter[]*<br>The SqlParameters to pass to the command |

#### Returns

A valid SqlCommand object

### CreateCommand(connection, spName, sourceColumns)

Simplify the creation of a Sql command object by allowing a stored procedure and optional parameters to be provided

#### Remarks

e.g.: SqlCommand command = CreateCommand(conn, "AddCustomer", "CustomerID", "CustomerName");

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection object |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| sourceColumns | *System.String[]*<br>An array of string to be assigned as the source columns of the stored procedure parameters |

#### Returns

A valid SqlCommand object

### CreateCommand(connectionString, commandText, commandType, commandParameters)

Simplify the creation of a Sql command object by allowing a stored procedure and optional parameters to be provided

#### Remarks

e.g.: SqlCommand command = CreateCommand(connenctionString, "AddCustomer", "CustomerID", "CustomerName");

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>A valid connection string for a SqlConnection |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>A valid SQL string to execute |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType to execute (i.e. StoredProcedure, Text) |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlParameter[]*<br>The SqlParameters to pass to the command |

#### Returns

A valid SqlCommand object

### CreateCommand(connectionString, spName, sourceColumns)

Simplify the creation of a Sql command object by allowing a stored procedure and optional parameters to be provided

#### Remarks

e.g.: SqlCommand command = CreateCommand(connenctionString, "AddCustomer", "CustomerID", "CustomerName");

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>A valid connection string for a SqlConnection |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| sourceColumns | *System.String[]*<br>An array of string to be assigned as the source columns of the stored procedure parameters |

#### Returns

A valid SqlCommand object

### DeriveParameters(cmd)

Calls the SqlCommandBuilder.DeriveParameters, doing any setup and cleanup necessary

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| cmd | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlCommand*<br>The SqlCommand referencing the stored procedure from which the parameter information is to be derived. The derived parameters are added to the Parameters collection of the SqlCommand. |

### ExecuteDataset(command)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the database specified in the connection string.

#### Remarks

e.g.: DataSet ds = ExecuteDataset(command);

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| command | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlCommand*<br>The SqlCommand to execute |

#### Returns

A dataset containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteDataset(connection, commandType, commandText, commandParameters)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the specified SqlConnection using the provided parameters.

#### Remarks

e.g.: DataSet ds = ExecuteDataset(conn, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders", new SqlParameter("@prodid", 24));

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or T-SQL command |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlParameter[]*<br>An array of SqlParamters used to execute the command |

#### Returns

A dataset containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteDataset(connection, commandType, commandText)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset and takes no parameters) against the provided SqlConnection.

#### Remarks

e.g.: DataSet ds = ExecuteDataset(conn, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders");

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or T-SQL command |

#### Returns

A dataset containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteDataset(connection, spName, parameterValues)

Execute a stored procedure via a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the specified SqlConnection using the provided parameter values. This method will query the database to discover the parameters for the stored procedure (the first time each stored procedure is called), and assign the values based on parameter order.

#### Remarks

This method provides no access to output parameters or the stored procedure's return value parameter. e.g.: DataSet ds = ExecuteDataset(conn, "GetOrders", 24, 36);

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| parameterValues | *System.Object[]*<br>An array of objects to be assigned as the input values of the stored procedure |

#### Returns

A dataset containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteDataset(transaction, commandType, commandText, commandParameters)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the specified SqlTransaction using the provided parameters.

#### Remarks

e.g.: DataSet ds = ExecuteDataset(trans, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders", new SqlParameter("@prodid", 24));

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| transaction | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlTransaction*<br>A valid SqlTransaction |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or T-SQL command |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlParameter[]*<br>An array of SqlParamters used to execute the command |

#### Returns

A dataset containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteDataset(transaction, commandType, commandText)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset and takes no parameters) against the provided SqlTransaction.

#### Remarks

e.g.: DataSet ds = ExecuteDataset(trans, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders");

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| transaction | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlTransaction*<br>A valid SqlTransaction |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or T-SQL command |

#### Returns

A dataset containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteDataset(transaction, spName, parameterValues)

This method will query the database to discover the parameters for the stored procedure (the first time each stored procedure is called), and assign the values based on parameter order.

#### Remarks

This method provides no access to output parameters or the stored procedure's return value parameter. e.g.: DataSet ds = ExecuteDataset(trans, "GetOrders", 24, 36);

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| transaction | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlTransaction*<br>A valid SqlTransaction |

### ExecuteDataset(connectionString, commandType, commandText, commandParameters)

| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |

| commandParameters | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlParameter[]*<br>An array of SqlParamters used to execute the command |

### ExecuteDataset(connectionString, commandType, commandText)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset and takes no parameters) against the database specified in the connection string.

#### Remarks
