### ExecuteDataset(connectionString, spName, parameterValues)

Execute a stored procedure via a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the database specified in the connection string using the provided parameter values. This method will query the database to discover the parameters for the stored procedure (the first time each stored procedure is called), and assign the values based on parameter order.

#### Remarks

This method provides no access to output parameters or the stored procedure's return value parameter. e.g.: DataSet ds = ExecuteDataset(connString, "GetOrders", 24, 36);

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>A valid connection string for a SqlConnection |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| parameterValues | *System.Object[]*<br>An array of objects to be assigned as the input values of the stored procedure |

#### Returns

A dataset containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteDatasetTypedParams(command, dataRow)

Execute a stored procedure via a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the database specified in the connection string using the dataRow column values as the stored procedure's parameters values. This method will assign the parameter values based on row values.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| command | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlCommand*<br>The SqlCommand to execute |
| dataRow | *System.Data.DataRow*<br>The dataRow used to hold the stored procedure's parameter values. |

#### Returns

A dataset containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteDatasetTypedParams(connection, spName, dataRow)

Execute a stored procedure via a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the specified SqlConnection using the dataRow column values as the store procedure's parameters values. This method will query the database to discover the parameters for the stored procedure (the first time each stored procedure is called), and assign the values based on row values.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection object |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| dataRow | *System.Data.DataRow*<br>The dataRow used to hold the stored procedure's parameter values. |

#### Returns

A dataset containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteDatasetTypedParams(transaction, spName, dataRow)

Execute a stored procedure via a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the specified SqlTransaction using the dataRow column values as the stored procedure's parameters values. This method will query the database to discover the parameters for the stored procedure (the first time each stored procedure is called), and assign the values based on row values.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| transaction | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlTransaction*<br>A valid SqlTransaction object |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| dataRow | *System.Data.DataRow*<br>The dataRow used to hold the stored procedure's parameter values. |

#### Returns

A dataset containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteDatasetTypedParams(connectionString, spName, dataRow)

Execute a stored procedure via a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the database specified in the connection string using the dataRow column values as the stored procedure's parameters values. This method will query the database to discover the parameters for the stored procedure (the first time each stored procedure is called), and assign the values based on row values.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>A valid connection string for a SqlConnection |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| dataRow | *System.Data.DataRow*<br>The dataRow used to hold the stored procedure's parameter values. |

#### Returns

A dataset containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteNonQuery(command)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns no resultset) against the database specified in the connection string

#### Remarks

e.g.: int result = ExecuteNonQuery(command);

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| command | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlCommand*<br>The SqlCommand to execute |

#### Returns

An int representing the number of rows affected by the command

### ExecuteNonQuery(connection, commandType, commandText, commandParameters)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns no resultset) against the specified SqlConnection using the provided parameters.

#### Remarks

e.g.: int result = ExecuteNonQuery(conn, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "PublishOrders", new SqlParameter("@prodid", 24));

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or T-SQL command |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlParameter[]*<br>An array of SqlParamters used to execute the command |

#### Returns

An int representing the number of rows affected by the command

### ExecuteNonQuery(connection, commandType, commandText)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns no resultset and takes no parameters) against the provided SqlConnection.

#### Remarks

e.g.: int result = ExecuteNonQuery(conn, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "PublishOrders");

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or T-SQL command |

#### Returns

An int representing the number of rows affected by the command

### ExecuteNonQuery(connection, spName, parameterValues)

Execute a stored procedure via a SqlCommand (that returns no resultset) against the specified SqlConnection using the provided parameter values. This method will query the database to discover the parameters for the stored procedure (the first time each stored procedure is called), and assign the values based on parameter order.

#### Remarks

This method provides no access to output parameters or the stored procedure's return value parameter. e.g.: int result = ExecuteNonQuery(conn, "PublishOrders", 24, 36);

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| parameterValues | *System.Object[]*<br>An array of objects to be assigned as the input values of the stored procedure |

#### Returns

An int representing the number of rows affected by the command

### ExecuteNonQuery(transaction, commandType, commandText, commandParameters)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns no resultset) against the specified SqlTransaction using the provided parameters.

#### Remarks

e.g.: int result = ExecuteNonQuery(trans, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders", new SqlParameter("@prodid", 24));

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| transaction | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlTransaction*<br>A valid SqlTransaction |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or T-SQL command |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlParameter[]*<br>An array of SqlParamters used to execute the command |

#### Returns

An int representing the number of rows affected by the command

### ExecuteScalar(command)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns a 1x1 resultset) against the database specified in the connection string.

#### Remarks

e.g.: int orderCount = (int)ExecuteScalar(command);

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| command | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlCommand*<br>The SqlCommand to execute |

#### Returns

An object containing the value in the 1x1 resultset generated by the command

| commandParameters | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlParameter[]*<br>An array of SqlParamters used to execute the command |

### ExecuteScalarTypedParams(command, dataRow)

Execute a stored procedure via a SqlCommand (that returns a 1x1 resultset) against the database specified in the connection string using the dataRow column values as the stored procedure's parameters values. This method will assign the parameter values based on parameter order.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| command | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlCommand*<br>The SqlCommand to execute |
| dataRow | *System.Data.DataRow*<br>The dataRow used to hold the stored procedure's parameter values. |

#### Returns

An object containing the value in the 1x1 resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteScalarTypedParams(connection, spName, dataRow)

Execute a stored procedure via a SqlCommand (that returns a 1x1 resultset) against the specified SqlConnection using the dataRow column values as the stored procedure's parameters values. This method will query the database to discover the parameters for the stored procedure (the first time each stored procedure is called), and assign the values based on parameter order.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection object |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| dataRow | *System.Data.DataRow*<br>The dataRow used to hold the stored procedure's parameter values. |

#### Returns

An object containing the value in the 1x1 resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteScalarTypedParams(transaction, spName, dataRow)

Execute a stored procedure via a SqlCommand (that returns a 1x1 resultset) against the specified SqlTransaction using the dataRow column values as the stored procedure's parameters values. This method will query the database to discover the parameters for the stored procedure (the first time each stored procedure is called), and assign the values based on parameter order.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| transaction | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlTransaction*<br>A valid SqlTransaction object |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| dataRow | *System.Data.DataRow*<br>The dataRow used to hold the stored procedure's parameter values. |

#### Returns

An object containing the value in the 1x1 resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteScalarTypedParams(connectionString, spName, dataRow)

Execute a stored procedure via a SqlCommand (that returns a 1x1 resultset) against the database specified in the connection string using the dataRow column values as the stored procedure's parameters values. This method will query the database to discover the parameters for the stored procedure (the first time each stored procedure is called), and assign the values based on parameter order.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>A valid connection string for a SqlConnection |

| dataRow | *System.Data.DataRow*<br>The dataRow used to hold the stored procedure's parameter values. |

#### Returns

An object containing the value in the 1x1 resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteXmlReader(command)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the provided SqlConnection.

#### Remarks

e.g.: XmlReader r = ExecuteXmlReader(SqlCommand command);

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| command | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlCommand*<br>The SqlCommand to execute |

#### Returns

An XmlReader containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteXmlReader(connection, commandType, commandText, commandParameters)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the specified SqlConnection using the provided parameters.

#### Remarks

e.g.: XmlReader r = ExecuteXmlReader(conn, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders", new SqlParameter("@prodid", 24));

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or T-SQL command using "FOR XML AUTO" |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlParameter[]*<br>An array of SqlParamters used to execute the command |

#### Returns

An XmlReader containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteXmlReader(connection, commandType, commandText)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset and takes no parameters) against the provided SqlConnection.

#### Remarks

e.g.: XmlReader r = ExecuteXmlReader(conn, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders");

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or T-SQL command using "FOR XML AUTO" |

#### Returns

An XmlReader containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteXmlReader(connection, spName, parameterValues)

Execute a stored procedure via a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the specified SqlConnection using the provided parameter values. This method will query the database to discover the parameters for the stored procedure (the first time each stored procedure is called), and assign the values based on parameter order.

#### Remarks

This method provides no access to output parameters or the stored procedure's return value parameter. e.g.: XmlReader r = ExecuteXmlReader(conn, "GetOrders", 24, 36);

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure using "FOR XML AUTO" |
| parameterValues | *System.Object[]*<br>An array of objects to be assigned as the input values of the stored procedure |

#### Returns

An XmlReader containing the resultset generated by the command

### ExecuteXmlReader(transaction, commandType, commandText, commandParameters)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the specified SqlTransaction using the provided parameters.

#### Remarks

e.g.: XmlReader r = ExecuteXmlReader(trans, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders", new SqlParameter("@prodid", 24));

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| transaction | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlTransaction*<br>A valid SqlTransaction |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or T-SQL command using "FOR XML AUTO" |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlParameter[]*<br>An array of SqlParamters used to execute the command |

#### Returns

An XmlReader containing the resultset generated by the command

An XmlReader containing the resultset generated by the command

#### Returns

A dataset containing the resultset generated by the command

### FillDataset(command, dataSet, tableNames)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the database specified in the connection string.

#### Remarks

e.g.: FillDataset(connString, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders", ds, new string[] {"orders"});

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| command | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlCommand*<br>The SqlCommand to execute |
| dataSet | *System.Data.DataSet*<br>A dataset wich will contain the resultset generated by the command |
| tableNames | *System.String[]*<br>This array will be used to create table mappings allowing the DataTables to be referenced by a user defined name (probably the actual table name) |

### FillDataset(connection, commandType, commandText, dataSet, tableNames, commandParameters)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset) against the specified SqlConnection using the provided parameters.

#### Remarks

e.g.: FillDataset(conn, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders", ds, new string[] {"orders"}, new SqlParameter("@prodid", 24));

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or T-SQL command |
| dataSet | *System.Data.DataSet*<br>A dataset wich will contain the resultset generated by the command |
| tableNames | *System.String[]*<br>This array will be used to create table mappings allowing the DataTables to be referenced by a user defined name (probably the actual table name) |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlParameter[]*<br>An array of SqlParamters used to execute the command |

### FillDataset(connection, commandType, commandText, dataSet, tableNames)

Execute a SqlCommand (that returns a resultset and takes no parameters) against the provided SqlConnection.

#### Remarks

e.g.: FillDataset(conn, CommandType.StoredProcedure, "GetOrders", ds, new string[] {"orders"});

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection |
| commandType | *System.Data.CommandType*<br>The CommandType (stored procedure, text, etc.) |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or T-SQL command |
| dataSet | *System.Data.DataSet*<br>A dataset wich will contain the resultset generated by the command |
| tableNames | *System.String[]*<br>This array will be used to create table mappings allowing the DataTables to be referenced by a user defined name (probably the actual table name) |

| parameterValues | *System.Object[]*<br>An array of objects to be assigned as the input values of the stored procedure |

### GetParameter(name, dbType, size, direction)

Get a SqlParameter for use in a SQL command

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| name | *System.String*<br>The name of the parameter to create |
| dbType | *System.Data.DbType*<br>The System.Data.DbType of the parameter |
| size | *System.Int32*<br>The size of the parameter |
| direction | *System.Data.ParameterDirection*<br>The System.Data.ParameterDirection of the parameter |

#### Returns

A SqlParameter object

### GetParameter(name, dbType, size, sourceColumn, sourceVersion)

Get a SqlParameter for use in a SQL command

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| name | *System.String*<br>The name of the parameter to create |
| dbType | *System.Data.DbType*<br>The System.Data.DbType of the parameter |
| size | *System.Int32*<br>The size of the parameter |
| sourceColumn | *System.String*<br>The source column of the parameter |
| sourceVersion | *System.Data.DataRowVersion*<br>The System.Data.DataRowVersion of the parameter |

A SqlParameter object

Get a SqlParameter for use in a SQL command

| ---- | ----------- |

| value | *System.Object*<br>The value of the specified parameter |

#### Returns

A SqlParameter object

### UpdateDataset(insertCommand, deleteCommand, updateCommand, dataSet, tableName, rowUpdating, rowUpdated)

Executes the System.Data.SqlClient.SqlCommand for each inserted, updated, or deleted row in the DataSet also implementing RowUpdating and RowUpdated Event Handlers

#### Remarks

e.g.: SqlRowUpdatingEventHandler rowUpdating = new SqlRowUpdatingEventHandler( OnRowUpdating ); SqlRowUpdatedEventHandler rowUpdated = new SqlRowUpdatedEventHandler( OnRowUpdated ); adoHelper.UpdateDataSet(sqlInsertCommand, sqlDeleteCommand, sqlUpdateCommand, dataSet, "Order", rowUpdating, rowUpdated);

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| insertCommand | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>A valid transact-SQL statement or stored procedure to insert new records into the data source |
| deleteCommand | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>A valid transact-SQL statement or stored procedure to delete records from the data source |
| updateCommand | *System.Data.IDbCommand*<br>A valid transact-SQL statement or stored procedure used to update records in the data source |
| dataSet | *System.Data.DataSet*<br>The DataSet used to update the data source |
| tableName | *System.String*<br>The DataTable used to update the data source. |
| rowUpdating | *Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.RowUpdatingHandler*<br>The AdoHelper.RowUpdatingEventHandler or null |
| rowUpdated | *Data4Net.Ado.AdoHelper.RowUpdatedHandler*<br>The AdoHelper.RowUpdatedEventHandler or null |

### UpdateDataset(insertCommand, deleteCommand, updateCommand, dataSet, tableName)

Executes the respective command for each inserted, updated, or deleted row in the DataSet.

#### Remarks

e.g.: UpdateDataset(conn, insertCommand, deleteCommand, updateCommand, dataSet, "Order");

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| insertCommand | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlCommand*<br>A valid transact-SQL statement or stored procedure to insert new records into the data source |
| deleteCommand | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlCommand*<br>A valid transact-SQL statement or stored procedure to delete records from the data source |
| updateCommand | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlCommand*<br>A valid transact-SQL statement or stored procedure used to update records in the data source |
| dataSet | *System.Data.DataSet*<br>The DataSet used to update the data source |
| tableName | *System.String*<br>The DataTable used to update the data source. |


## SqlHelperParameterCache

SqlHelperParameterCache provides functions to leverage a static cache of procedure parameters, and the ability to discover parameters for stored procedures at run-time.

### CacheParameterSet(connectionString, commandText, commandParameters)

Add parameter array to the cache

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>A valid connection string for a SqlConnection |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or T-SQL command |
| commandParameters | *System.Data.SqlClient.SqlParameter[]*<br>An array of SqlParamters to be cached |

### GetCachedParameterSet(connectionString, commandText)

Retrieve a parameter array from the cache

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>A valid connection string for a SqlConnection |
| commandText | *System.String*<br>The stored procedure name or T-SQL command |

#### Returns

An array of SqlParamters

### GetSpParameterSet(connection, spName, includeReturnValueParameter)

Retrieves the set of SqlParameters appropriate for the stored procedure

#### Remarks

This method will query the database for this information, and then store it in a cache for future requests.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.IDbConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection object |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| includeReturnValueParameter | *System.Boolean*<br>A bool value indicating whether the return value parameter should be included in the results |

#### Returns

An array of SqlParameters

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if spName is null

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if connection is null

### GetSpParameterSet(connection, spName)

Retrieves the set of SqlParameters appropriate for the stored procedure

#### Remarks

This method will query the database for this information, and then store it in a cache for future requests.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connection | *System.Data.IDbConnection*<br>A valid SqlConnection object |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |

#### Returns

An array of SqlParameters

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if spName is null

*System.ArgumentNullException:* Thrown if connection is null

### GetSpParameterSet(connectionString, spName, includeReturnValueParameter)

Retrieves the set of SqlParameters appropriate for the stored procedure

#### Remarks

This method will query the database for this information, and then store it in a cache for future requests.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>A valid connection string for a SqlConnection |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |
| includeReturnValueParameter | *System.Boolean*<br>A bool value indicating whether the return value parameter should be included in the results |

#### Returns

An array of SqlParameters

### GetSpParameterSet(connectionString, spName)

Retrieves the set of SqlParameters appropriate for the stored procedure

#### Remarks

This method will query the database for this information, and then store it in a cache for future requests.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| connectionString | *System.String*<br>A valid connection string for a SqlConnection |
| spName | *System.String*<br>The name of the stored procedure |

#### Returns

An array of SqlParameters

### DeclareReturnParameter(name)

## BaseModuleRewriter

The base class for module rewriting. This class is abstract, and therefore must be derived from.

#### Remarks

Provides the essential base functionality for a rewriter using the HttpModule approach.

### Constructor



### BaseModuleRewriter_AuthorizeRequest(System.Object,System.EventArgs)

Called when the module's AuthorizeRequest event fires.

#### Remarks

This event handler calls the <a href="#basemodulerewriter.rewrite(system.string,system.web.httpapplication)">BaseModuleRewriter.Rewrite(System.String,System.Web.HttpApplication)</a> method, passing in the  and HttpApplication passed in via the  parameter.

### Dispose



### Init(app)

Executes when the module is initialized.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| app | *System.Web.HttpApplication*<br>A reference to the HttpApplication object processing this request. |

#### Remarks

Wires up the HttpApplication's AuthorizeRequest event to the <a href="#basemodulerewriter.basemodulerewriter_authorizerequest(system.object,system.eventargs)">BaseModuleRewriter.BaseModuleRewriter_AuthorizeRequest(System.Object,System.EventArgs)</a> event handler.

### Rewrite(requestedPath, app)

The  method must be overriden. It is where the logic for rewriting an incoming URL is performed.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| requestedPath | *System.String*<br>The requested RawUrl. (Includes full path and querystring.) |
| app | *System.Web.HttpApplication*<br>The HttpApplication instance. |


## RewriterConfigSerializerSectionHandler

Deserializes the markup in Web.config into an instance of the <a href="#rewriterconfiguration">RewriterConfiguration</a> class.

### Create(System.Object,System.Object,System.Xml.XmlNode)

Creates an instance of the <a href="#rewriterconfiguration">RewriterConfiguration</a> class.

#### Remarks

Uses XML Serialization to deserialize the XML in the Web.config file into an <a href="#rewriterconfiguration">RewriterConfiguration</a> instance.

#### Returns

An instance of the <a href="#rewriterconfiguration">RewriterConfiguration</a> class.


## RewriterConfiguration

Specifies the configuration settings in the Web.config for the RewriterRule.

#### Remarks

This class defines the structure of the Rewriter configuration file in the Web.config file. Currently, it allows only for a set of rewrite rules; however, this approach allows for customization. For example, you could provide a ruleset that  use regular expression matching; or a set of constant names and values, which could then be referenced in rewrite rules.  The structure in the Web.config file is as follows: 
```

            <configuration>
            	<configSections>
            		<section name="RewriterConfig" 
            		            type="URLRewriter.Config.RewriterConfigSerializerSectionHandler, URLRewriter" />
            	</configSections>
            	
            	<RewriterConfig>
            		<Rules>
            			<RewriterRule>
            				<LookFor>pattern</LookFor>
            				<SendTo>replace with</SendTo>
            			</RewriterRule>
            			<RewriterRule>
            				<LookFor>pattern</LookFor>
            				<SendTo>replace with</SendTo>
            			</RewriterRule>
            			...
            			<RewriterRule>
            				<LookFor>pattern</LookFor>
            				<SendTo>replace with</SendTo>
            			</RewriterRule>
            		</Rules>
            	</RewriterConfig>
            	
            	<system.web>
            		...
            	</system.web>
            </configuration>
            
```


### GetConfig

GetConfig() returns an instance of the  class with the values populated from the Web.config file. It uses XML deserialization to convert the XML structure in Web.config into a  instance.

#### Returns

A <a href="#rewriterconfiguration">RewriterConfiguration</a> instance.

### Rules

A <a href="#rewriterrulecollection">RewriterRuleCollection</a> instance that provides access to a set of <a href="#rewriterrule">RewriterRule</a>s.


## RewriterRule

Represents a rewriter rule. A rewriter rule is composed of a pattern to search for and a string to replace the pattern with (if matched).

### LookFor

Gets or sets the pattern to look for.

#### Remarks

 is a regular expression pattern. Therefore, you might need to escape characters in the pattern that are reserved characters in regular expression syntax (., ?, ^, $, etc.).  The pattern is searched for using the  class's  method. The pattern is case insensitive.

### SendTo

The string to replace the pattern with, if found.

#### Remarks

The replacement string may use grouping symbols, like $1, $2, etc. Specifically, the  class's  method is used to replace the match in <a href="#rewriterrule.lookfor">RewriterRule.LookFor</a> with the value in .


## RewriterRuleCollection

The RewriterRuleCollection models a set of RewriterRules in the Web.config file.

#### Remarks

The RewriterRuleCollection is expressed in XML as: 
```

            <RewriterRule>
              <LookFor>pattern to search for</LookFor>
              <SendTo>string to redirect to</LookFor>
            <RewriterRule>
            <RewriterRule>
              <LookFor>pattern to search for</LookFor>
              <SendTo>string to redirect to</LookFor>
            <RewriterRule>
            ...
            <RewriterRule>
              <LookFor>pattern to search for</LookFor>
              <SendTo>string to redirect to</LookFor>
            <RewriterRule>
            
```


### Add(r)

Adds a new RewriterRule to the collection.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| r | *Data4Net.URLRewriter.Config.RewriterRule*<br>A RewriterRule instance. |

### Item(System.Int32)

Gets or sets a RewriterRule at a specified ordinal index.

## RewriterFactoryHandler

Provides an HttpHandler that performs redirection.

#### Remarks

The RewriterFactoryHandler checks the rewriting rules, rewrites the path if needed, and then delegates the responsibility of processing the ASP.NET page to the  class (the same one used by the  class).

### GetHandler(context, requestType, url, pathTranslated)

GetHandler is executed by the ASP.NET pipeline after the associated HttpModules have run. The job of GetHandler is to return an instance of an HttpHandler that can process the page.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| context | *System.Web.HttpContext*<br>The HttpContext for this request. |
| requestType | *System.String*<br>The HTTP data transfer method ( or ) |
| url | *System.String*<br>The RawUrl of the requested resource. |
| pathTranslated | *System.String*<br>The physical path to the requested resource. |

#### Returns

An instance that implements IHttpHandler; specifically, an HttpHandler instance returned by the  class, which is the same class that the default ASP.NET PageHandlerFactory delegates to.

### ReleaseHandler(handler)



| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| handler | *System.Web.IHttpHandler*<br> |

### ResolveUrl(appPath, url)

Converts a URL into one that is usable on the requesting client.

#### Remarks

Converts ~ to the requesting application path. Mimics the behavior of the  method, which is often used by control developers.

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| appPath | *System.String*<br>The application path. |
| url | *System.String*<br>The URL, which might contain ~. |

#### Returns

A resolved URL. If the input parameter  contains ~, it is replaced with the value of the  parameter.

### _keyList

### AddData\`\`1(key, targetObject, cacheSeconds, isAddKeyList)

Add cache, 将指定项添加到 Cache 对象，该对象具有依赖项、过期和优先级策略以及一个委托（可用于在从 Cache 移除插入项时通知应用程序）。如果 Cache 中已保存了具有相同 key 参数的项，则对此方法的调用将失败。若要使用相同的 key 参数改写现有的 Cache 项，请使用 Insert 方法。

#### Type Parameters

- T - 

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| key | *System.String*<br> |
| targetObject | *\`\`0*<br> |
| cacheSeconds | *System.Double*<br>Seconds, -1 is forever |
| isAddKeyList | *System.Boolean*<br> |

#### Returns



### AddData\`\`1(key, targetObject, cacheSeconds)

## LoginSsoLocalHelper

LoginSsoLocalHelper Class  First Redirect Url: http://localhost/LoginSsoLocal.aspx?appId=100001ZIelVNmOrriG&urlback=http://localhost/a.asp&urlencode=gb2312  Second Redirect Url: http://localhost/a.asp?appId=xxxx&timer=xxxx  Thrid Redirect Url: http://localhost/LoginSsoLocal.aspx?data=xxxx&appId=100001&vkey=xxxx&urlencode=gb2312&md5type=asp  Suggest MD5 key length is greater than 20.  MD5: data + appId + timer + key

### _LoginSsoLocalXmlDoc

xml配置文件

| dPhase | *System.Double*<br>波形的起始相位，取值区间[0-2*PI) |

#### Returns




## ValidateCodeImg2

验证码图片生成类 ValidateCodeImg2 （仅做代码参考，请勿使用！）  1） 生成验证码图片（见ValidateCodeImg.aspx文件），用户请求此aspx文件时会返回图片。  2） 在Html中添加对该图片的引用  3） 验证用户输入的验证码是否正确 

#### Remarks

_CodeShowMode可以控制显示的复杂度，1最容易，2中等，3最难，3对性能要求较高，建议1或2 _CodeShowFontSpace可以控制字符间距，越小字符连接越紧密，自动程序分割更加困难，同时人眼识别难度也会增加 其他参数项见下面的注释说明

### GetHtml(ctrl)

Get HTML by controls  当在GridView中使用，需要做如下设置 1. 首先重载VerifyRenderingInServerForm方法 public override void VerifyRenderingInServerForm(Control control) { //当使用GridView时，不能使用 //base.VerifyRenderingInServerForm(control); } 2. 设置EnableEventValidation属性 public override bool EnableEventValidation { get { //当使用GridView时，return false //return base.EnableEventValidation; return false; } set { base.EnableEventValidation = value; } } 或 在web.config中修改<pages enableEventValidation="false"></pages> 或 <%@ Page Language="C#" EnableEventValidation="false" AutoEventWireup="true" CodeFile="ExportGridView.aspx.cs" Inherits="ExportGridView" %>

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| ctrl | *System.Web.UI.Control*<br> |

#### Returns

### LocalAddr

得到服务器IP地址, if null or object is null, return string.Empty

### MainUrl

得到本地 https://www.microsoft.com:8080, 如果current不是web系统返回empty

### MainUrlApplicationPath

得到本地, 如: http://www.microsoft.com https://www.microsoft.com:8080 http://www.microsoft.com:8080/Web 如果current不是web系统返回empty

### RawUrl

得到当前原始Url

### RawUrlQueryString

通过当前原始Url得到原始QueryString

### RawUrlQuestionQueryString

通过当前原始Url得到原始QueryString, 如不为空, 则开头包含"?"符号

### RawUrlWithAll

得到当前原始Url, 完整版, 包含域名端口等信息

### RedirectJs(url)

Redirect by javascript

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| url | *System.String*<br> |

### RemoteAddr

得到客户IP地址, if null or object is null, return string.Empty

### ResponseAddHeader_P3P

解决跨域Session丢失问题 P3P : CP=CAO PSA OUR

### ResponseAddHeader_P3P2

解决跨域Session丢失问题 P3P : CP="NOI ADM DEV PSAi COM NAV OUR OTR STP IND DEM"

### ResponseFile(fileContent, fileName, fileType, isAttachment)

输出文件

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| fileContent | *System.String*<br>文件内容 |
| fileName | *System.String*<br>文件名字，如2007-07-28.doc, 2007-07-28.xls, Pv.txt等 |
| fileType | *System.String*<br>文件类型 可以为application/ms-excel application/ms-word application/ms-txt application/ms-html 或其他浏览器可直接支持文档 "text/plain"用于作为文本内容返回而不是已解释的 HTML 语句 如果含有中文，并在Excel中打开会乱码，请把 "<meta content='text/html; charset=utf-8' http-epuiv='content-type'/>" + fileContent 之前 |
| isAttachment | *System.Boolean*<br>是否已附件形式下载 |

### ScriptName

得到页面文件地址,即虚拟地址

### ServerName

得到server name, 如www.microsoft.com, 如果current不是web系统返回empty

#### Returns



### ServerPort

得到端口号, 如:8080 :80 :443, 如果current不是web系统返回empty

#### Returns

| ---- | ----------- |

### SessionIDStrong

### UrlReferrer

### GetWeekOfYear_ZeroToLast(dt, weekOfFirstDay)

取指定日期是一年中的第几周 (把今年开始几天（非7天）算作上一年的最后一周，且返回上一年的这周周几)

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| dt | *System.DateTime*<br>指定日期 |
| weekOfFirstDay | *System.Int32*<br>每个星期的开始第一天是星期几 (0,Sunday...6,Saturday) |

#### Returns



### GetWeekOfYear(dt, weekOfFirstDay, isZeroWeek)

取指定日期是一年中的第几周

| Name | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| dt | *System.DateTime*<br>指定日期 |
| weekOfFirstDay | *System.Int32*<br>每个星期的开始第一天是星期几 (0,Sunday...6,Saturday) |
| isZeroWeek | *System.Boolean*<br>是否把今年开始几天（非7天）算作上一年的最后一周 true: 今年开始剩余天数算今年第0周 false: 今年开始剩余天数算今年第1周 |

#### Returns
